<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">1979–80 UEFA Cup</h1>
<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
<div id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
<div id="contentSub"></div>
<div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">
					Jump to:					<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, 					<a href="#p-search">search</a>
</div>
<div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en"><script>function mfTempOpenSection(id){var block=document.getElementById("mf-section-"+id);block.className+=" open-block";block.previousSibling.className+=" open-block";}</script><p>The <b>1979–80 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UEFA_Cup" title="UEFA Cup">UEFA Cup</a></b> was won by <a href="/wiki/Eintracht_Frankfurt" title="Eintracht Frankfurt">Eintracht Frankfurt</a> on away goals over <a href="/wiki/Borussia_M%C3%B6nchengladbach" title="Borussia Mönchengladbach">Borussia Mönchengladbach</a>. The tournament was notable for all four semi-finalists coming from Germany, with a 5th being eliminated in the quarter-finals. This is the only time all the semifinalists came from one nation.</p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Third_round">Third round</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1979%E2%80%9380_UEFA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Third round">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="wikitable" style="text-align:center">
<tr>
<th style="text-align:right; width:250px">Team 1</th>
<th style="width:80px"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Aggregate_score" title="Aggregate score"><abbr title="Aggregate score">Agg.</abbr></a></th>
<th style="text-align:left; width:250px">Team 2</th>
<th style="width:80px">1st leg</th>
<th style="width:80px">2nd leg</th>
</tr>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Second_leg_3">Second leg</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1979%E2%80%9380_UEFA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Second leg">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<p><i>Dynamo Kyiv 2–2 Lokomotiv Sofia on aggregate. Lokomotiv Sofia won on away goals rule.</i></p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Second_leg_4">Second leg</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1979%E2%80%9380_UEFA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Second leg">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="vevent" style="width: 100%; background-color: transparent; clear:both">
<p><span class="summary" style="display: none;"><a href="/wiki/PFC_Lokomotiv_Sofia" title="PFC Lokomotiv Sofia">Lokomotiv Sofia</a> <span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Bulgaria" title="Bulgaria"><img alt="Bulgaria" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="1000" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cc/Flag_of_Bulgaria_%281971_%E2%80%93_1990%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_Bulgaria_%281971_%E2%80%93_1990%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cc/Flag_of_Bulgaria_%281971_%E2%80%93_1990%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_Bulgaria_%281971_%E2%80%93_1990%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cc/Flag_of_Bulgaria_%281971_%E2%80%93_1990%29.svg/46px-Flag_of_Bulgaria_%281971_%E2%80%93_1990%29.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> v <span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/West_Germany" title="West Germany"><img alt="West Germany" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="1000" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/23px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/35px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/46px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vfb_Stuttgart" title="Vfb Stuttgart">Stuttgart</a></span></p>

<td>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Second_leg_6">Second leg</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1979%E2%80%9380_UEFA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Second leg">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

</tr>
</table>
<table style="float:left; width:24%; table-layout:fixed">
<tr>
<td>
<div style="font-size: 85%"><span class="location"><a href="/wiki/Commerzbank-Arena" title="Commerzbank-Arena">Waldstadion</a>, <a href="/wiki/Frankfurt" title="Frankfurt">Frankfurt</a></span><br/>
Attendance: 59,000<br/>
Referee: <a href="/wiki/Alexis_Ponnet" title="Alexis Ponnet">Alexis Ponnet</a> (<a href="/wiki/Royal_Belgian_Football_Association" title="Royal Belgian Football Association">Belgium</a>)</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
</div>
<p><i>Eintracht Frankfurt 3–3 Borussia Mönchengladbach on aggregate. Lokomotiv Sofia won on away goals rule.</i></p>
